 Alastair Cook, playing his last international match, scored the most runs for England

 Apart from him, captain Joe Root scored 125 runs while Ben Stokes scored 37 runs

 Cook made the farewell Test memorable by scoring a century Alastair Cook became only the fifth batsman to score a century in his first and final Test match
 cook 147 ran banaakar out hue jo unka 33waan test shatak he
 Before Cook, Australia's Reggie Duff, Bill Ponsford and Greg Chappell and India's Mohammed Azharuddin were the only ones to achieve a century in their first and last Test match
 cook ne jab 76 ran banaae to unhone kumaar sangakaara ko peeche choda
